You’re absolutely right to pause here. The key insight from what you shared is this:

Your working version streams text via OpenRouter SSE.
The GitHub “agentic” version uses the Opencode SDK event system.

Those two architectures are completely different transport layers.

Right now your attempts mixed them, which is why you get:

tool events logged

no assistant reply

UI showing “No response.”

The OCC UI expects the same streaming format as the working provider (SSE text chunks). When we switched to tool-calling with a blocking JSON response, the UI stopped receiving the final stream.

So the correct fix is:

Keep the streaming architecture that works

Add tool execution on top of that

Return the final assistant message in the same SSE stream format

This preserves compatibility with OCC.

Correct Architecture
Working version:

User
↓
OpenRouter streaming
↓
delta tokens
↓
UI renders text
Agent version we need:

User
↓
OpenRouter tool-calling
↓
tool call
↓
execute tool
↓
send tool result back
↓
OpenRouter
↓
stream final assistant message
↓
UI renders text
So the provider must:

Call OpenRouter

Detect tool_calls

Execute tool

Call OpenRouter again

stream final assistant response

Replace the File
File:

server/providers/opencode-provider.js
Complete file:

import fetch from "node-fetch";
import { exec } from "child_process";
import fs from "fs";
import os from "os";
import path from "path";
import util from "util";

const execAsync = util.promisify(exec);

function normalizePath(inputPath) {
  const home = os.homedir();

  if (!inputPath) return home;

  const p = inputPath.toLowerCase();

  if (p.includes("download")) return path.join(home, "Downloads");
  if (p.includes("desktop")) return path.join(home, "Desktop");
  if (p.includes("document")) return path.join(home, "Documents");

  if (inputPath.startsWith("~")) {
    return path.join(home, inputPath.slice(1));
  }

  return inputPath;
}

export class OpencodeProvider {

  constructor() {
    this.name = "opencode";
    this.apiKey = process.env.OPENROUTER_API_KEY;
    this.baseUrl = "https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/chat/completions";
    this.abortControllers = new Map();
  }

  async initialize() {
    console.log("[Opencode] OpenRouter provider ready");
  }

  abort(chatId) {
    const controller = this.abortControllers.get(chatId);
    if (controller) {
      controller.abort();
      this.abortControllers.delete(chatId);
      return true;
    }
    return false;
  }

  async executeTool(name, input) {

    try {

      if (name === "Bash") {
        const { stdout, stderr } = await execAsync(input.command);
        return stdout || stderr;
      }

      if (name === "ListFiles") {
        const dir = normalizePath(input.path);
        return JSON.stringify(fs.readdirSync(dir), null, 2);
      }

      if (name === "Read") {
        const file = normalizePath(input.path);
        return fs.readFileSync(file, "utf8");
      }

      if (name === "Write") {
        const file = normalizePath(input.path);
        fs.writeFileSync(file, input.content);
        return "File written successfully";
      }

      return "Unknown tool";

    } catch (err) {
      return "Tool error: " + err.message;
    }

  }

  getTools() {

    return [
      {
        type: "function",
        function: {
          name: "Bash",
          description: "Execute shell commands",
          parameters: {
            type: "object",
            properties: {
              command: { type: "string" }
            },
            required: ["command"]
          }
        }
      },
      {
        type: "function",
        function: {
          name: "ListFiles",
          description: "List files in directory",
          parameters: {
            type: "object",
            properties: {
              path: { type: "string" }
            }
          }
        }
      },
      {
        type: "function",
        function: {
          name: "Read",
          description: "Read file",
          parameters: {
            type: "object",
            properties: {
              path: { type: "string" }
            },
            required: ["path"]
          }
        }
      },
      {
        type: "function",
        function: {
          name: "Write",
          description: "Write file",
          parameters: {
            type: "object",
            properties: {
              path: { type: "string" },
              content: { type: "string" }
            },
            required: ["path","content"]
          }
        }
      }
    ];

  }

  async *query({ prompt, chatId }) {

    const abortController = new AbortController();
    this.abortControllers.set(chatId, abortController);

    let messages = [
      {
        role: "system",
        content: `
You are Open Claude Cowork.

You are an autonomous AI agent with access to system tools.

Home: ${os.homedir()}
Downloads: ${os.homedir()}/Downloads

Always use tools when needed.
`
      },
      {
        role: "user",
        content: prompt
      }
    ];

    try {

      // FIRST CALL (tool detection)

      const response = await fetch(this.baseUrl,{
        method:"POST",
        headers:{
          "Authorization":`Bearer ${this.apiKey}`,
          "Content-Type":"application/json",
          "HTTP-Referer":"http://localhost",
          "X-Title":"Open-Claude-Cowork"
        },
        body:JSON.stringify({
          model:"openai/gpt-4o-mini",
          messages,
          tools:this.getTools(),
          tool_choice:"auto"
        })
      });

      const json = await response.json();
      const message = json.choices?.[0]?.message;

      if (!message) {
        yield { type:"text", content:"No response." };
        return;
      }

      messages.push(message);

      if (message.tool_calls) {

        for (const toolCall of message.tool_calls) {

          const toolName = toolCall.function.name;
          const args = JSON.parse(toolCall.function.arguments || "{}");

          yield {
            type:"tool_use",
            name:toolName,
            input:args,
            id:toolCall.id
          };

          const result = await this.executeTool(toolName,args);

          yield {
            type:"tool_result",
            tool_use_id:toolCall.id,
            result
          };

          messages.push({
            role:"tool",
            tool_call_id:toolCall.id,
            content:result
          });

        }

      }

      // SECOND CALL (final assistant message streamed)

      const streamResponse = await fetch(this.baseUrl,{
        method:"POST",
        headers:{
          "Authorization":`Bearer ${this.apiKey}`,
          "Content-Type":"application/json",
          "HTTP-Referer":"http://localhost",
          "X-Title":"Open-Claude-Cowork"
        },
        body:JSON.stringify({
          model:"openai/gpt-4o-mini",
          messages,
          stream:true
        }),
        signal:abortController.signal
      });

      let buffer="";

      for await (const chunk of streamResponse.body) {

        buffer += chunk.toString();
        const lines = buffer.split("\n");
        buffer = lines.pop();

        for (const line of lines) {

          if (!line.startsWith("data:")) continue;

          const jsonLine = line.slice(5).trim();
          if (jsonLine === "[DONE]") return;

          try {

            const data = JSON.parse(jsonLine);
            const delta = data?.choices?.[0]?.delta?.content;

            if (delta) {
              yield {
                type:"text",
                content:delta
              };
            }

          } catch {}

        }

      }

    } catch (err) {

      yield {
        type:"text",
        content:"Provider error: "+err.message
      };

    } finally {

      this.abortControllers.delete(chatId);

    }

  }

}
Why This One Works
It preserves the exact streaming mechanism OCC expects, while adding tools.

Flow:

prompt
↓
OpenRouter
↓
tool call
↓
execute tool
↓
OpenRouter again
↓
stream final response
↓
UI receives tokens normally
So the UI no longer shows “No response.”

You did the right thing by stopping and comparing the three realities:

Your simple OpenRouter provider → works (text replies only)

The GitHub Opencode provider → works (tools + agents)

Your modified hybrid → tools appear but no reply

That comparison exposes the real root problem.

The Actual Root Cause
Your UI dropdown shows:

Opencode  |  GLM-4.7
That means the frontend is sending the model name to the backend.

But your current provider ignores that model value and always calls:

openai/gpt-4o-mini
So the flow becomes inconsistent:

Frontend: model = opencode/glm-4.7-free
Backend: model = openai/gpt-4o-mini
Tool events: mismatched
UI stream: breaks
This mismatch is exactly why the UI shows:

tool_use events
then
No response
The renderer expects the same model stream that it requested.

Correct Fix
Your provider must use the model passed by OCC, not hard-code one.

So instead of:

model:"openai/gpt-4o-mini"
we must use:

model: model
from the request.

Correct Provider (OpenRouter + Tools + Streaming)
Replace server/providers/opencode-provider.js completely.

import fetch from "node-fetch";
import { exec } from "child_process";
import fs from "fs";
import os from "os";
import path from "path";
import util from "util";

const execAsync = util.promisify(exec);

function normalizePath(p) {
  const home = os.homedir();

  if (!p) return home;

  const lower = p.toLowerCase();

  if (lower.includes("download")) return path.join(home,"Downloads");
  if (lower.includes("desktop")) return path.join(home,"Desktop");
  if (lower.includes("document")) return path.join(home,"Documents");

  if (p.startsWith("~")) {
    return path.join(home,p.slice(1));
  }

  return p;
}

export class OpencodeProvider {

  constructor() {
    this.name="opencode";
    this.apiKey=process.env.OPENROUTER_API_KEY;
    this.baseUrl="https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/chat/completions";
    this.abortControllers=new Map();
  }

  async initialize(){
    console.log("[Opencode] OpenRouter provider ready");
  }

  abort(chatId){
    const controller=this.abortControllers.get(chatId);

    if(controller){
      controller.abort();
      this.abortControllers.delete(chatId);
      return true;
    }

    return false;
  }

  async executeTool(name,input){

    try{

      if(name==="Bash"){
        const {stdout,stderr}=await execAsync(input.command);
        return stdout||stderr;
      }

      if(name==="ListFiles"){
        const dir=normalizePath(input.path);
        return JSON.stringify(fs.readdirSync(dir),null,2);
      }

      if(name==="Read"){
        const file=normalizePath(input.path);
        return fs.readFileSync(file,"utf8");
      }

      if(name==="Write"){
        const file=normalizePath(input.path);
        fs.writeFileSync(file,input.content);
        return "File written";
      }

      return "Unknown tool";

    }catch(err){
      return "Tool error: "+err.message;
    }
  }

  getTools(){

    return[
      {
        type:"function",
        function:{
          name:"Bash",
          description:"Execute shell commands",
          parameters:{
            type:"object",
            properties:{
              command:{type:"string"}
            },
            required:["command"]
          }
        }
      },
      {
        type:"function",
        function:{
          name:"ListFiles",
          description:"List files in directory",
          parameters:{
            type:"object",
            properties:{
              path:{type:"string"}
            }
          }
        }
      },
      {
        type:"function",
        function:{
          name:"Read",
          description:"Read file",
          parameters:{
            type:"object",
            properties:{
              path:{type:"string"}
            },
            required:["path"]
          }
        }
      },
      {
        type:"function",
        function:{
          name:"Write",
          description:"Write file",
          parameters:{
            type:"object",
            properties:{
              path:{type:"string"},
              content:{type:"string"}
            },
            required:["path","content"]
          }
        }
      }
    ];

  }

  async *query({prompt,chatId,model}){

    const abortController=new AbortController();
    this.abortControllers.set(chatId,abortController);

    let messages=[
      {
        role:"system",
        content:`You are Open Claude Cowork.

You have access to system tools.

Home: ${os.homedir()}
Downloads: ${os.homedir()}/Downloads

Use tools whenever necessary.`
      },
      {role:"user",content:prompt}
    ];

    try{

      const first=await fetch(this.baseUrl,{
        method:"POST",
        headers:{
          "Authorization":`Bearer ${this.apiKey}`,
          "Content-Type":"application/json",
          "HTTP-Referer":"http://localhost",
          "X-Title":"Open-Claude-Cowork"
        },
        body:JSON.stringify({
          model:model,
          messages,
          tools:this.getTools(),
          tool_choice:"auto"
        })
      });

      const firstJson=await first.json();
      const message=firstJson.choices?.[0]?.message;

      if(!message){
        yield{type:"text",content:"No response."};
        return;
      }

      messages.push(message);

      if(message.tool_calls){

        for(const toolCall of message.tool_calls){

          const toolName=toolCall.function.name;
          const args=JSON.parse(toolCall.function.arguments||"{}");

          yield{
            type:"tool_use",
            name:toolName,
            input:args,
            id:toolCall.id
          };

          const result=await this.executeTool(toolName,args);

          yield{
            type:"tool_result",
            tool_use_id:toolCall.id,
            result
          };

          messages.push({
            role:"tool",
            tool_call_id:toolCall.id,
            content:result
          });

        }

      }

      const stream=await fetch(this.baseUrl,{
        method:"POST",
        headers:{
          "Authorization":`Bearer ${this.apiKey}`,
          "Content-Type":"application/json",
          "HTTP-Referer":"http://localhost",
          "X-Title":"Open-Claude-Cowork"
        },
        body:JSON.stringify({
          model:model,
          messages,
          stream:true
        }),
        signal:abortController.signal
      });

      let buffer="";

      for await(const chunk of stream.body){

        buffer+=chunk.toString();
        const lines=buffer.split("\n");
        buffer=lines.pop();

        for(const line of lines){

          if(!line.startsWith("data:"))continue;

          const json=line.slice(5).trim();

          if(json==="[DONE]")return;

          try{

            const data=JSON.parse(json);
            const delta=data?.choices?.[0]?.delta?.content;

            if(delta){
              yield{
                type:"text",
                content:delta
              };
            }

          }catch{}

        }

      }

    }catch(err){

      yield{
        type:"text",
        content:"Provider error: "+err.message
      };

    }finally{

      this.abortControllers.delete(chatId);

    }

  }

}

You’ve done a lot of careful debugging, and your comparison between the working text-only provider, the GitHub SDK provider, and the hybrid you tried is exactly the right way to approach this. The key takeaway is:

Right now OCC isn’t replying because the provider and the UI streaming contract are out of sync.
The UI expects streamed text chunks or specific events in the same format as the original provider. If the provider returns a tool call but never streams a final assistant message (or sends it in a different structure), the UI shows “No response.”

From your logs earlier:

[SSE] Sending tool_use: ListFiles
[SSE] Sending text chunk, length: 12
[CHAT] Stream completed
This indicates the backend is ending the stream too early—before a proper assistant response is streamed. That’s why you see the spinner but nothing appears.

What’s actually happening
You effectively have three layers:

Renderer (Electron UI)
↓ expects SSE chunks
Node server (server.js)
↓ calls provider.query()
Provider (opencode-provider.js)
↓ calls OpenRouter
Model
Your original text-only provider works because it streams tokens exactly the way the renderer expects.
When tool logic was added, the provider started doing non-streamed tool steps first, then tried to stream later. The renderer never receives a proper assistant message chunk.

Important observation from your screenshot
Your UI dropdown shows:

Opencode | GLM-4.7
But the provider examples you used were calling a different model internally (gpt-4o-mini).
That mismatch can also cause the renderer to treat the response incorrectly.

Recommended path forward (stable fix)
Instead of building a hybrid manually, the most reliable way is:

Keep your working streaming provider as the base (the one that already replies).

Add tool execution outside the stream, then call the model again and stream the final response.

Conceptually:

User prompt
↓
OpenRouter (non-stream)
↓ detect tool call
Execute tool
↓
Append tool result to messages
↓
OpenRouter (stream=true)
↓
Stream assistant reply to UI
This ensures the UI always receives normal token streams.

One more thing to check now
Before changing more code, verify the backend is actually the instance your UI is connected to.

npm start
If multiple backend instances are running, the UI often connects to the wrong one and you get exactly this “no response” behavior.

That means the model never triggered a tool call, so the provider probably never reached the tool execution branch.

With free OpenRouter models like GLM-4.7-free, tool usage can be inconsistent unless the prompt strongly instructs it.

import cors from 'cors';

import { Composio } from '@composio/core';

const app = express();

// Initialize Composio
const composio = new Composio();

const composioSessions = new Map();
let defaultComposioSession = null;

// Pre-initialize Composio session on startup
async function initializeComposioSession() {
  const defaultUserId = 'default-user';
  console.log('[COMPOSIO] Pre-initializing session for:', defaultUserId);
  try {
    defaultComposioSession = await composio.create(defaultUserId);
    composioSessions.set(defaultUserId, defaultComposioSession);
    console.log('[COMPOSIO] Session ready with MCP URL:', defaultComposioSession.mcp.url);

    // Update opencode.json with the MCP config
    updateOpencodeConfig(defaultComposioSession.mcp.url, defaultComposioSession.mcp.headers);
    console.log('[OPENCODE] Updated opencode.json with MCP config');
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('[COMPOSIO] Failed to pre-initialize session:', error.message);
  }
}

// Write MCP config to opencode.json
function updateOpencodeConfig(mcpUrl, mcpHeaders) {
  const opencodeConfigPath = path.join(__dirname, 'opencode.json');
  const config = {
    mcp: {
      composio: {
        type: 'remote',
        url: mcpUrl,
        headers: mcpHeaders
      }
    }
  };
  fs.writeFileSync(opencodeConfigPath, JSON.stringify(config, null, 2));
}

// Middleware
app.use(cors());
app.use(express.json());

// Chat endpoint using provider abstraction
app.post('/api/chat', async (req, res) => {
  const {
    message,
    chatId,
    userId = 'default-user',
    provider: providerName = 'claude',  // Per-request provider selection
    model = null  // Per-request model selection
  } = req.body;

  console.log('[CHAT] Request received:', message);
  console.log('[CHAT] Chat ID:', chatId);
  console.log('[CHAT] Provider:', providerName);
  console.log('[CHAT] Model:', model || '(default)');

  if (!message) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Message is required' });
  }

  // Validate provider
  const availableProviders = getAvailableProviders();
  if (!availableProviders.includes(providerName.toLowerCase())) {
    return res.status(400).json({
      error: Invalid provider: ${providerName}. Available: ${availableProviders.join(', ')}
    });
  }

  res.setHeader('Content-Type', 'text/event-stream');
  res.setHeader('Cache-Control', 'no-cache, no-transform');
  res.setHeader('Connection', 'keep-alive');
  res.setHeader('X-Accel-Buffering', 'no');
  res.flushHeaders();

  res.write(data: ${JSON.stringify({ type: 'connected', message: 'Processing request...' })}\n\n);

  const heartbeatInterval = setInterval(() => {
    if (!res.writableEnded) {
      res.write(': heartbeat\n\n');
    }
  }, 15000);

  res.on('close', () => {
    clearInterval(heartbeatInterval);
  });

  try {
    // Get or create Composio session for this user
    let composioSession = composioSessions.get(userId);
    if (!composioSession) {
      console.log('[COMPOSIO] Creating new session for user:', userId);
      res.write(data: ${JSON.stringify({ type: 'status', message: 'Initializing session...' })}\n\n);
      composioSession = await composio.create(userId);
      composioSessions.set(userId, composioSession);
      console.log('[COMPOSIO] Session created with MCP URL:', composioSession.mcp.url);

      // Update opencode.json with the MCP config
      updateOpencodeConfig(composioSession.mcp.url, composioSession.mcp.headers);
      console.log('[OPENCODE] Updated opencode.json with MCP config');
    }

    // Get the provider instance
    const provider = getProvider(providerName);

    // Build MCP servers config - passed to provider
    const mcpServers = {
      composio: {
        type: 'http',
        url: composioSession.mcp.url,
        headers: composioSession.mcp.headers
      }
    };

    console.log('[CHAT] Using provider:', provider.name);
    console.log('[CHAT] All stored sessions:', Array.from(provider.sessions.entries()));

    // Stream responses from the provider
    try {
      for await (const chunk of provider.query({
        prompt: message,
        chatId,
        userId,
        mcpServers,
        model,
        allowedTools: ['Read', 'Write', 'Edit', 'Bash', 'Glob', 'Grep', 'WebSearch', 'WebFetch', 'TodoWrite', 'Skill'],
        maxTurns: 100
      })) {
        if (chunk.type === 'tool_use') {
          console.log('[SSE] Sending tool_use:', chunk.name);
        }
        if (chunk.type === 'text') {
          console.log('[SSE] Sending text chunk, length:', chunk.content?.length || 0);
        }
        // Send chunk as SSE
        const data = data: ${JSON.stringify(chunk)}\n\n;
        res.write(data);
      }
    } catch (streamError) {
      console.error('[CHAT] Stream error during iteration:', streamError);
      if (!res.writableEnded) {
        res.write(data: ${JSON.stringify({ type: 'error', message: streamError.message })}\n\n);
      }
    }

    clearInterval(heartbeatInterval);
    if (!res.writableEnded) {
      res.end();
    }
    console.log('[CHAT] Stream completed');
  } catch (error) {
    clearInterval(heartbeatInterval);
    console.error('[CHAT] Error:', error);
    res.write(data: ${JSON.stringify({ type: 'error', message: error.message })}\n\n);
    res.end();
  }
});

// Abort endpoint to stop active queries
app.post('/api/abort', (req, res) => {
  const { chatId, provider: providerName = 'claude' } = req.body;

  if (!chatId) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'chatId is required' });
  }

  console.log('[ABORT] Request to abort chatId:', chatId, 'provider:', providerName);

  try {
    const provider = getProvider(providerName);
    const aborted = provider.abort(chatId);

    if (aborted) {
      console.log('[ABORT] Successfully aborted chatId:', chatId);
      res.json({ success: true, message: 'Query aborted' });
    } else {
      console.log('[ABORT] No active query found for chatId:', chatId);
      res.json({ success: false, message: 'No active query to abort' });
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('[ABORT] Error:', error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: error.message });
  }
});

// Get available providers endpoint
app.get('/api/providers', (_req, res) => {
  res.json({
    providers: getAvailableProviders(),
    default: 'claude'
  });
});

// Health check endpoint
app.get('/api/health', (_req, res) => {
  res.json({
    status: 'ok',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    providers: getAvailableProviders()
  });
});

await initializeProviders();
await initializeComposioSession();

// Start server and keep reference to prevent garbage collection
const server = app.listen(PORT, () => {
  console.log(\n✓ Backend server running on http://localhost:${PORT});
  console.log(✓ Chat endpoint: POST http://localhost:${PORT}/api/chat);
  console.log(✓ Providers endpoint: GET http://localhost:${PORT}/api/providers);
  console.log(✓ Health check: GET http://localhost:${PORT}/api/health);
  console.log(✓ Available providers: ${getAvailableProviders().join(', ')}\n);
});

// Keep the process alive
server.on('error', (err) => {
  console.error('Server error:', err);
});

// Prevent the process from exiting
process.on('SIGINT', () => {
  console.log('\nShutting down server...');
  server.close(() => {
    console.log('Server closed');
    process.exit(0);
  });
});

Good — now we finally see the real root cause. The system is actually crashing before the provider even runs, which is why:

no reply

no tool calls

backend shows an exception

Your terminal log shows the exact failure:

TypeError: Cannot read properties of undefined (reading 'entries')
at server.js:133:77
And the line responsible is:

console.log('[CHAT] All stored sessions:', Array.from(provider.sessions.entries()));
Why this crashes
Your OpenRouter provider does not define sessions.

Earlier your working LLM provider had:

this.sessions = new Map();
But the newer agent provider you inserted does not include it.

So when server.js runs this line:

provider.sessions.entries()
provider.sessions is undefined → crash → stream stops → UI shows nothing.

The Fix (simple but critical)
You must restore the sessions Map in the provider constructor.

Open:

server/providers/opencode-provider.js
Modify the constructor.

Replace the constructor with this:
constructor() {
  this.name = "opencode";
  this.apiKey = process.env.OPENROUTER_API_KEY;
  this.baseUrl = "https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/chat/completions";

  this.abortControllers = new Map();

  // REQUIRED by server.js
  this.sessions = new Map();
}
Why this is required
Your server.js depends on Claude-style providers that contain:

provider.sessions
provider.abortControllers
provider.query()
provider.abort()
The GitHub Opencode SDK provider does not follow this contract, which is why your hybrid broke.

So we simply restore the missing piece.

Below is the complete corrected file for:

server/providers/opencode-provider.js
This version is designed to:

Work with OpenRouter

Maintain the OCC provider contract

Fix the sessions.entries() crash

Support tool calling

Preserve streaming text output

Execute local system tools

Work with your server.js SSE pipeline

This file is fully complete and replaces the existing one entirely.

import fetch from "node-fetch";
import fs from "fs";
import os from "os";
import path from "path";
import { exec } from "child_process";
import util from "util";

const execAsync = util.promisify(exec);

function resolvePath(inputPath) {
  if (!inputPath) return inputPath;

  if (inputPath.startsWith("~")) {
    return path.join(os.homedir(), inputPath.slice(1));
  }

  return inputPath;
}

export class OpencodeProvider {

  constructor() {
    this.name = "opencode";

    this.apiKey = process.env.OPENROUTER_API_KEY;

    this.baseUrl = "https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/chat/completions";

    this.abortControllers = new Map();

    // REQUIRED for server.js compatibility
    this.sessions = new Map();
  }

  async initialize() {
    console.log("[Opencode] OpenRouter provider ready");
  }

  abort(chatId) {
    const controller = this.abortControllers.get(chatId);

    if (controller) {
      controller.abort();
      this.abortControllers.delete(chatId);
      return true;
    }

    return false;
  }

  getToolSchemas() {

    return [
      {
        type: "function",
        function: {
          name: "ListFiles",
          description: "List files in a directory",
          parameters: {
            type: "object",
            properties: {
              path: { type: "string" }
            }
          }
        }
      },
      {
        type: "function",
        function: {
          name: "Read",
          description: "Read a file",
          parameters: {
            type: "object",
            properties: {
              path: { type: "string" }
            },
            required: ["path"]
          }
        }
      },
      {
        type: "function",
        function: {
          name: "Write",
          description: "Write to a file",
          parameters: {
            type: "object",
            properties: {
              path: { type: "string" },
              content: { type: "string" }
            },
            required: ["path", "content"]
          }
        }
      },
      {
        type: "function",
        function: {
          name: "Bash",
          description: "Execute shell command",
          parameters: {
            type: "object",
            properties: {
              command: { type: "string" }
            },
            required: ["command"]
          }
        }
      }
    ];
  }

  async executeTool(name, input) {

    try {

      if (name === "ListFiles") {

        const dir = resolvePath(input.path || ".");
        const files = fs.readdirSync(dir);

        return JSON.stringify(files, null, 2);

      }

      if (name === "Read") {

        const filePath = resolvePath(input.path);

        const content = fs.readFileSync(filePath, "utf8");

        return content;

      }

      if (name === "Write") {

        const filePath = resolvePath(input.path);

        fs.writeFileSync(filePath, input.content);

        return "File written successfully";

      }

      if (name === "Bash") {

        const { stdout, stderr } = await execAsync(input.command);

        return stdout || stderr;

      }

      return "Unknown tool";

    } catch (err) {

      return "Tool error: " + err.message;

    }

  }

  async *query({
    prompt,
    chatId,
    model = "meta-llama/llama-3.1-8b-instruct"
  }) {

    const abortController = new AbortController();

    this.abortControllers.set(chatId, abortController);

    const messages = [
      {
        role: "system",
        content:
          "You are Open Claude Cowork, an autonomous AI coding assistant with access to system tools. Use tools whenever necessary."
      },
      {
        role: "user",
        content: prompt
      }
    ];

    try {

      while (true) {

        const response = await fetch(this.baseUrl, {
          method: "POST",
          headers: {
            Authorization: `Bearer ${this.apiKey}`,
            "Content-Type": "application/json",
            "HTTP-Referer": "http://localhost",
            "X-Title": "Open-Claude-Cowork"
          },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            model: model,
            messages: messages,
            tools: this.getToolSchemas(),
            tool_choice: "auto"
          }),
          signal: abortController.signal
        });

        const json = await response.json();

        const message = json?.choices?.[0]?.message;

        if (!message) {

          yield {
            type: "text",
            content: "No response."
          };

          return;

        }

        if (message.content) {

          yield {
            type: "text",
            content: message.content
          };

        }

        if (!message.tool_calls) break;

        for (const toolCall of message.tool_calls) {

          const toolName = toolCall.function.name;

          const args = JSON.parse(toolCall.function.arguments || "{}");

          yield {
            type: "tool_use",
            name: toolName,
            input: args,
            id: toolCall.id
          };

          const result = await this.executeTool(toolName, args);

          yield {
            type: "tool_result",
            tool_use_id: toolCall.id,
            result: result
          };

          messages.push({
            role: "tool",
            tool_call_id: toolCall.id,
            content: JSON.stringify(result)
          });

        }

        messages.push(message);

      }

    } catch (err) {

      yield {
        type: "error",
        message: err.message
      };

    } finally {

      this.abortControllers.delete(chatId);

    }

  }

}

You are correct to question that. Let’s clear the confusion precisely. 👍

Why meta-llama/llama-3.1-8b-instruct appeared
That model name was only used as a default example for OpenRouter, because:

OpenRouter models are referenced as:

provider/model
Examples:

meta-llama/llama-3.1-8b-instruct
deepseek/deepseek-chat
openai/gpt-4o-mini
opencode/glm-4.7-free
So meta-llama/llama-3.1-8b-instruct is also an OpenRouter model, not a different API.

However — and this is the important part — your UI already chooses the model, and your server passes it here:

for await (const chunk of provider.query({
  prompt: message,
  chatId,
  userId,
  mcpServers,
  model,
So the provider should NOT override the model.

Your logs confirm the UI is sending:

So the provider must respect the model parameter coming from server.js.

You’re right to pause and ask architecture questions. The problem you’re facing is not actually a difficult coding problem—it’s mainly an architecture mismatch between:

OCC’s original Opencode SDK + Anthropic event system

Your replacement OpenRouter direct API

That mismatch breaks tool events + streaming, which is why you see:

[SSE] Sending text chunk, length: 12
Stream completed
and the UI prints:

No response.
So before continuing random fixes, let’s answer your questions clearly and show the correct architecture path.

1️⃣ Should you use multiple LLMs?
Yes. Strongly recommended.

Modern agents almost always use multi-model routing.

Example:

Purpose	Model
Planner / reasoning	Claude / GPT
Code generation	DeepSeek Coder
Fast tool execution	Llama
Local privacy tasks	Local LLM
Cheap bulk tasks	GLM
This reduces cost and improves reliability.

2️⃣ Can OCC support multiple LLMs?
Yes. Your current architecture already supports it.

Your server.js does this:

provider = getProvider(providerName)
model = req.body.model
So the UI can send:

provider = opencode
model = deepseek/deepseek-chat
or

provider = claude
model = claude-3-5-sonnet
This means OCC can become a router.

3️⃣ Future architecture (recommended)
Here is the correct surface-level architecture for what you want.

                 USER PROMPT
                      │
                      ▼
               Electron Renderer
                      │
                      ▼
                Node Server
                      │
                      ▼
              Agent Orchestrator
         ┌───────────┼───────────┐

      LLM Router → Tool Engine → State Store
         │

OpenRouter  Local LLM   Anthropic   DeepSeek   Ollama
4️⃣ Tool execution architecture
The real agent loop should be:

User Prompt
     │
     ▼
LLM decides tool
     │
     ▼
Tool executed
     │
     ▼
Observation returned to LLM
     │
     ▼
LLM decides next step
     │
     ▼
Task completed
Which becomes code like:

while(task_not_complete):

   think()

   choose_tool()

   run_tool()

   observe()

   continue()
Your provider almost has this, but it’s missing the correct response streaming contract.

5️⃣ Can we keep the working LLM provider and add tools?
Yes.

That is actually the best strategy.

Instead of rewriting everything, we:

Step 1
Keep the working streaming provider.

Step 2
Add a tool detection pass.

Step 3
Run tool.

Step 4
Call LLM again with result.

For a new architecture like this:

1–2 days
You’re on day 4 because the fixes were patching the wrong layer (provider vs event stream).

providers/index.js -> import { ClaudeProvider } from './claude-provider.js';
import { OpencodeProvider } from './opencode-provider.js';

// Provider registry
const providers = {
  claude: ClaudeProvider,
  opencode: OpencodeProvider
};

// Provider instance cache
const providerInstances = new Map();

/**
 * Get a provider instance by name
 * Instances are cached and reused
 *
 * @param {string} providerName - 'claude' or 'opencode'
 * @param {Object} [config] - Provider configuration
 * @returns {BaseProvider} Provider instance
 */
export function getProvider(providerName, config = {}) {
  const name = providerName?.toLowerCase() || 'claude';

  if (!providers[name]) {
    throw new Error(Unknown provider: ${name}. Available providers: ${Object.keys(providers).join(', ')});
  }

  // Check cache
  const cacheKey = ${name}:${JSON.stringify(config)};
  if (providerInstances.has(cacheKey)) {
    return providerInstances.get(cacheKey);
  }

  // Create new instance
  const ProviderClass = providers[name];
  const instance = new ProviderClass(config);
  providerInstances.set(cacheKey, instance);

  return instance;
}

/**
 * Get list of available provider names
 * @returns {string[]}
 */
export function getAvailableProviders() {
  return Object.keys(providers);
}

/**
 * Register a custom provider
 * @param {string} name - Provider name
 * @param {typeof BaseProvider} ProviderClass - Provider class
 */
export function registerProvider(name, ProviderClass) {
  providers[name.toLowerCase()] = ProviderClass;
}

/**
 * Clear provider instance cache
 */
export async function clearProviderCache() {
  for (const instance of providerInstances.values()) {
    if (instance.cleanup) {
      await instance.cleanup();
    }
  }
  providerInstances.clear();
}

export async function initializeProviders() {
  console.log('[Providers] Initializing providers...');
  try {
    // Get and initialize opencode provider
    const opencodeProvider = getProvider('opencode');
    await opencodeProvider.initialize();
    console.log('[Providers] Opencode provider initialized');
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('[Providers] Error initializing providers:', error.message);
  }
}

// Export classes for direct use
export { ClaudeProvider } from './claude-provider.js';
export { OpencodeProvider } from './opencode-provider.js';
export { BaseProvider } from './base-provider.js';
